Networks for kata1
==================

Here are stats and download links for all the neural networks from this run.

If you are a casual user, you want "Network File" - you can directly use this .bin.gz file with [KataGo](https://github.com/lightvector/KataGo/releases).

The neural network files and weights on this page are covered by this [license](https://katagotraining.org/network_license/), except for the oldest networks near the bottom of this page that are marked by their name as being imported from the older "g170" run, which are under [CC0](https://creativecommons.org/publicdomain/zero/1.0/).

Elo ratings are approximate and are \*not\* necessarily comparable to the Elos from any other bot or run. Uncertainty radius displayed is approximately two sigmas.
